Reuters, London, 12th. The number of unemployed people in the United Kingdom continues to increase. According to this week's statistics, the number of unemployed people has increased by another 25,000, reaching a total of 2,263,000 people.

Rubber Trees in Dutch East Indies Cut Down in Preparation for Planting Rice

Reuters, Paris, Batavia, 12th. On the west coast of Sumatra in the Dutch East Indies, locals who plant rubber trees have begun to cut down rubber trees in preparation for planting rice due to the current low price of rubber.

National News

The Capital Holds

Premier's Birthday Commemoration

The Central Party Headquarters held a Premier's Birthday Commemoration ceremony at the auditorium at 8:00 AM on the 12th. Attendees included Chiang Kai-shek, Tai Chuan-hsien, Ho Ying-chin, Hu Han-min, Sun Fo, Chen Mingshu, Ye Chucang, Chu Pei-teh, Wu Zhihui, Yu Youren, Song Ziwen, He Chengjun, Li Wenfan, Ding Chao Wu, Wang Boling, Shao Yuanchong, Zhu Jiahua, Zhang Qun, Liu Zhi, Yang Shuzhuang, Zhou Qigang, Chen Lifu, Chen Zhaoying, Liu Jiwen, Liu Luyin, Ding Weifen, Zeng Yangfu, Fang Juehui, Wang Zhengting, Chen Yaoyuan, Zhang Zhen, Kong Xiangxi, Liu Wendao, Zhang Daofan, Gui Chongji, Yu Jingtang, Jiao Yitang, Ma Chaojun, Chen Ce, Miao Peicheng, Cheng Tianfang, Ke Xinge, Wu Jingheng, Zhang Renjie, Lin Sen, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Wang Chonghui, Shao Lizi, Li Yuying, En Ke Ba Gu, Chen Bulei, Lin Yungai, Ming Qingyang, and Zhang Xueliang, Zhu Guangmu and Central Party Headquarters staff, totaling over 600 people. After Chairman Hu Hanmin led the ceremony, he delivered a speech stating that the significance of commemorating the Premier's birthday today is extremely profound. All nations solemnly commemorate the birthdays of great martyrs and sages. Our commemoration of the Premier's birthday is to remember the Premier's great achievements and be faithful followers of the Premier. The Premier was the creator of the Three Principles of the People in the world. The day of the Premier's birth is also the day of the birth of the Three Principles of the People. In thousands of years of history, both Chinese and foreign, there has never been such a great personality and great doctrine. Europe and America consider Napoleon and Washington as great figures. The Chinese used to admire them as well, but after the Three Principles of the People, it is felt that Napoleon only had military achievements and, apart from knowing nationalism, did not think much about democracy and people's livelihood. As for Washington, his achievements are indeed greater than Napoleon's, but when Washington created the United States, the population was only seven or eight million, compared to the Premier's creation of the Republic of China with 400 million people. The difficulty and magnitude of their achievements are different. Moreover, Washington only broke away from British independence and did not determine any doctrine, so his spirit cannot be as great as the Premier's. As for Marx's theories, they were revised rather than created. Therefore, the Premier's Three Principles of the People are indeed a doctrine that can lead the world. Our commemoration of the Premier's birthday is to remember the Premier's achievements and continue the Premier's work, so that we can demonstrate the significance of commemorating the Premier. The Premier's thinking does not dwell on the past or the present, but seeks progress in the future. This is the Premier's greatest teaching. We commemorate the birthday by following this great teaching and putting it into practice. The Premier's teachings have three "musts": "must awaken the people," "must follow what I have written..." and "must realize it in the shortest possible time." If these three "musts" are not fully achieved, the revolution has not yet succeeded. Therefore, we should continue to work hard and fight together. We must put the Premier's teachings into practice and seek progress in the future. Everyone must view it this way to commemorate the Premier's birthday and never forget this kind of commemoration. Next, Wu Jingheng gave a speech stating that the Premier's physical body concluded after sixty-five years, but the Premier's spirit will live on with the world. The Republic of China created by the Premier will also live on with the world. The Three Principles of the People created by the Premier are the great law of the world. The great laws of the past five thousand years in the world have not been complete until the Premier's time. Imperialism has become a thing of the past, and the principle of people's livelihood is the savior of the present. Ordinary people wish others a hundred years of life, but I wish the Three Principles of the People ten thousand years of life, and the great harmony of the world five hundred million years of life. I wish the Premier's spirit to live on with the world. After the speech, the meeting adjourned.

The National Government held a Premier's Birthday Commemoration ceremony at the auditorium at 10:30 AM. Attendees included Chiang Kai-shek, Hu Hanmin, Tai Jitao, Zhang Xueliang, Lin Sen, Zhu Peide, Song Ziwen, Yang Shuzhuang, He Yingqin, Wang Chonghui, Ma Fuxiang, He Yaotsu, Yi Peiji, Kong Xiangxi, Zhang Qun, Wang Zhengting, Chen Yi, and the heads of various yuan, ministries, and commissions, as well as officials and military attachés from the National Government, totaling over 600 people. After Chairman Chiang Kai-shek led the ceremony, he delivered an opening speech stating that today is the Premier's birthday, which is also the day of the birth of the Party's doctrine. Since the Premier's death, the Party's Three Principles of the People and the Premier's life's work have been entirely entrusted to us to continue. Therefore, the future of the Three Principles of the People and the Premier's life depends on the efforts of our comrades. Today, in commemorating the Premier, I hope that everyone will not only follow the Premier's will, but also follow the Premier's "peaceful struggle to save China" and continue to work hard. I deeply hope that after the military ends, everyone will unite to respect the Premier's will and make a great determination to create a clean government. If we can do this, the Three Principles of the People can be realized. I hope everyone will encourage each other. In the future, anyone who makes mistakes should be strictly corrected. Even if I, Chiang Kai-shek, make mistakes, I hope everyone will strictly supervise me so that we can achieve the goal of true construction. Next, Tai Jitao gave a speech stating that today's commemoration of the Premier's birthday coincides with the complete elimination of reactionary forces. The country has entered a clear period. In this period, commemorating the Premier's birthday, I deeply believe that the Premier's spirit and doctrine will be further promoted, so that the whole country can be influenced by the doctrine and strive to build in accordance with the Premier's doctrine. I just heard Chairman Chiang's instructions, hoping that from now on, under the leadership of the Premier's doctrine, we will earnestly carry out the various undertakings outlined in the National Construction Program, especially hoping that appropriate talents will be appointed to appropriate positions in the government, so that everyone can concentrate on their work to fulfill the purpose of everyone being able to use their talents to the fullest. Chairman Chiang appropriately said that he hopes to create a clean government. I would like to add that in addition to creating a clean government, we should also create a capable government, so that capable talents can work hard for a capable government. After Tai's speech, Chairman Chiang said that Commander Zhang Hanqing has arrived in the capital to participate in the Premier's Birthday Commemoration, and he would like to take this opportunity to introduce Commander Zhang to give a speech. After Chiang's announcement, the audience applauded thunderously. Zhang Xueliang then took the stage amidst applause and said that he was honored to be ordered by the Chairman to say a few words. Xueliang has not made any contributions or achievements to the Party and the country, but he is deeply ashamed of the government's generous treatment. Today, in commemorating the Premier's birthday, we truly believe that the Premier's personality is great and that all the work he did was for the country and the people, not for personal gain. Therefore, everyone respects the Premier's personality. Xueliang believes that if we can all follow what the Premier did, we will naturally have a clean government and a clean country to seek happiness for the people. After Zhang's speech, the music was played and the meeting adjourned.

The Capital's various circles held a celebration ceremony for the Premier's Birthday at the public sports field at 9:00 AM. Representatives from all levels of the Party headquarters, various institutions, groups, and the public, totaling over 10,000 people, attended. Shi Weihuan was elected as chairman to lead the ceremony. Gu Zhenglun raised the flag, and several airplanes released leaflets in the sky. The chairman delivered an opening speech stating that the Premier's birth sixty-five years ago was the day of the birth of national salvation for the whole world. The Premier, seeing the corruption of the Qing government, created a revolution and overthrew the autocratic politics of more than 4,000 years. His great achievements are recorded in history. The ancients considered establishing virtue, establishing speech, and establishing meritorious service as immortal achievements. The Premier embodied all three in one person. In the 20th century world, he is truly the greatest of mankind, and it can be said that he has no predecessor and no successor. Our admiration for the Premier cannot be expressed by words alone. We must always respect the Premier's great personality, abide by his teachings, and implement the Three Principles of the People as the government's political goal to show that the Premier's spirit is always present. Vice Commander Zhang arrived in the capital today and hopes to sincerely support the central government and assist in building a new Republic of China. Then the future history must be more glorious. Next, Zhu Wenzhong, representative of the National Government, and Chen Haicheng, representative of the Legislative Yuan, also gave speeches. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM.

Liao Zhang Leaves Yingkou and Shenyang Southbound

Central representatives Wu Tiecheng and Liu Guang and others traveled together. Shi Yousan went to Tianjin on the same day, claiming to have reached a satisfactory agreement.

Shenyang Correspondence: There were rumors that Zhang Xueliang would meet Commander-in-Chief Chiang in Tianjin, Peiping, Qingdao, or Nanjing. A few days ago, it was decided to meet in Qingdao, and staff were sent to prepare the headquarters and arrange all security matters. Finally, after two contacts by Wu Tiecheng, it was decided to meet in the capital. Zhang's departure special train was ordered by the Beining Railway Bureau two days ago to prepare two trains. The first train had a pistol team, guard battalion, communications company, six cars, two military trucks, and various military supplies. The second train was Zhang's special train. The cars were divided into five groups: general affairs, secretary, staff, adjutant, and military supply. The military supply office was temporarily added. The head of the general affairs office was Zhu Guangmu (Director of the Northeast Telecommunications Administration). The head of the secretariat was Ye Biliang (Secretary of the Northeast Frontier Defense Commander's Office). The head of the staff office was Bao Wenye (Director of the Special Zone Police Department). The head of the adjutant's office was Huang Xiansheng (Commander of the 20th Brigade of the Northeast Army). The head of the military supply office was Su Quanbin. The above five offices are all temporary in nature, and the staff have not been separately appointed. Central representatives Wu Tiecheng, Liu Guang, Zhang Ji, and He Fenglin and others traveled along, all riding in the second train. Most of the attendants in the special train brought their families, so there was a lot of luggage. There were a total of twenty-three cars, decorated with new paint. Most of the cars were made of steel and were very heavy, so each train was towed by three locomotives. The special train was fired up at about 5:00 PM on the 7th. The servants and other personnel serving on the train also boarded the train separately to arrange everything. At 8:00 PM, the attendants were ordered to board the train one after another. The first train left at 10:00 PM to clear the way. At the same time, from Zhang Xueliang's residence to the new Shenyang station, the road was full of military police, with strict security. The new station, Laodaokou, and Huanggu Tun station were all the responsibility of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. The area near the Liaoning General Station was the responsibility of the Third Branch of the Commercial Port Public Security Bureau. Zhang arrived at the station at 10:30 PM. Military and political leaders all went to the station to see him off. After Zhang boarded the train, as the train headed west, military music played loudly. After the train left the station, the send-offs dispersed. Zhang's itinerary is to first arrive in Tianjin, stay there for a day or two, and then transfer to the Jinpu Railway to the south to pay respects to the tomb of the late Premier, meet Commander-in-Chief Chiang, and attend the Fourth Plenary Session, before heading north to Peiping to preside over the aftermath. Zhang's trip will take at least two weeks before he can return to Shenyang. The security of Shenyang is extremely important. At this time, when the Northeast Communists are lurking and plotting, it is especially necessary for someone to preside over it. Therefore, Zhang has entrusted all military and political powers to Zhang Zuoxiang, Chairman of Jilin Province.

Before Vice Commander Zhang Xueliang left Shenyang, Shi Yousan, commander of the Thirteenth Route Army, prepared to return to Shunhe. Shi's negotiation of pay and defense areas was satisfactory. On the 7th at noon, Shi's special train was fired up. His attendants and guards were all ready. The guards boarded the train first. At 3:00 PM, Shi and many attendants arrived at the station. The Frontier Defense Commissioner's Office sent a military band and a garrison team to provide security and escort. Zhang Zuoxiang, Chairman of Jilin Province, Wan Fulin, Chairman of Jiang Province, Zhang Jinghui, Administrative Chief of the Special Zone, Liu Shangqing, Committee Member of the Northeast Political Committee, Wang Shuhan, Secretary-General of the Frontier Defense, Rong Zhen, Director of the Military Department, Zhou Lian, Director of the Military Supply Department, Yang Zhengzhi, Director of the Adjutant Department, Ji Jinchun, Councilor, Yan Chaoxi, Liu Duoquan, Commander of the Guards, Wang Yizhe, Commander of the First Brigade, and Sun Xuchang, Director of the Police Department, all went to the station to see him off. When the dignitaries arrived at the station, they were separately welcomed onto the train to rest. Before long, Zhang Xueliang also arrived at the station to see Shi off, accompanied by his bodyguard adjutant Tan Hai in car number 1385. Zhang and Shi talked briefly on the train. Zhang then took the dignitaries who were seeing him off on the train and got off the train together. Shi shook hands and thanked Zhang and the other personnel before boarding the train and heading west. Zhang Xueliang and Zhang Zuoxiang rode in the same car back to the residence. Shi's adjutant chief Sun Tieling and Bi Guangyuan, the former committee member of Shandong Province, did not travel together because they were ordered by Shi to set up the Thirteenth Route Army Liaison Office in Shenyang. Sun and others moved from Wan Fulin's private residence to the Zhaodai Office on Sanjing Road on the evening of the 6th. According to Shi's interview with reporters, the results of this trip were extremely satisfactory. After arriving in Tianjin, he plans to stay for a day or two to meet with Chairman Wang Shuchang, and then go to Peiping to meet with Garrison Commander Yu Xuezhong before returning to his defense area. He Yingqin Returns to Jin from Zhengzhou

He Talks to the Press About the Situation in Yu and Shaanxi

He Yingqin, Minister of Military and Political Affairs and Director of the Zhengzhou Headquarters, returned to Jin by plane from Zhengzhou at 1:15 PM yesterday (10th). A reporter from the Central News Agency went to visit and had the following conversation with He: The reporter asked, "When will the minister leave Zhengzhou, and will he have to go to the front again in the future?" He replied, "I left Zhengzhou at 9:30 AM today. This time, I am accompanying Commander-in-Chief Sun Lianzhong to Jin to visit Commander-in-Chief Chiang and meet with Vice Commander Zhang, and to participate in the opening ceremony of the Fourth Plenary Session. I will probably stay in Jin for three or four days before returning to the front." The reporter asked, "What is the situation of Feng and Yan's troops now?" He replied, "Feng's generals, such as Ji Hongchang, Liang Guanying, Sun Lianzhong, Zhang Yinxiang, Ge Yunlong, and Zhang Zhan, have long disapproved of Feng's actions and have sincerely supported the central government in seeking national unification. However, at that time, they were held hostage by Feng and could do nothing. Therefore, as soon as they had the opportunity, they came to surrender. The rest, such as Zhang Weixi, Tian Jinkai, Feng Zhi'an, and Ming Baoshan, with a total of about 60,000 to 70,000 troops, have all been surrounded and disarmed by the central army in Xinzheng. As for Liu Yufen of Shaanxi, he was indeed captured alive by the troops under Commander-in-Chief Yang Hucheng. Song Zheyuan's whereabouts are unknown and it is heard that he has died in the chaos. The troops that are now following Feng in southern Jin are only a few thousand new recruits without guns recruited by Liu Zhen and the remnants of Pang Bingxun's troops, and of course they will no longer pose a problem. As for Yan Xishan's troops, they never had any combat capability. After suffering repeated defeats on the Longhai and Jinpu lines, they had already lost more than half of their strength. They then planned to retreat to Shanxi to linger on. Seeing that the situation was gone and there was no way to recover, they issued a telegram on the fourth day of the month, claiming to have been strictly ordered to supervise his departure and return to the fields, seemingly still wanting to live in Shanxi, holding the army hostage to protect his territory. His warlord's mind and feudal thoughts are unbreakable. However, the Shanxi army has no fighting spirit, and Niangziguan is far less dangerous than Tongguan. As long as the central army attacks, it can be resolved in the shortest possible time." The reporter asked, "What is the situation in Henan?" He replied, "Henan has suffered greatly due to the war, and Feng's rebels have wantonly plundered it, leading to the decline of democracy. Since Feng's defeat, local order has gradually been restored." The reporter asked, "I heard that the minister flew to Xi'an to inspect. What are your thoughts?" He replied, "Since the recovery of Xi'an, Feng's troops have been completely resolved. However, bandits have risen up and harassed the local area, and Zhen Turen's troops have the worst reputation. Commander-in-Chief Yang has captured and executed Zhen. Now he has sent troops to suppress them everywhere, and order can be restored. Over the years, Feng has ravaged and plundered Shaanxi without leaving any trace, and natural disasters have occurred frequently, and famine has struck repeatedly. The suffering of the people of Shaanxi is the worst in the country. It is said that in Wugong County, which originally had a population of 150,000, more than 80,000 people starved to death in one year. The corpses were piled up and no one cared about them. There were also thousands of disaster victims who wanted to escape from Xi'an to the border of Henan. Because the residents along the way lacked food and had no way to beg, they all starved to death on the way. The situation was extremely tragic. The people of Shaanxi have been under the oppression of warlords for a long time, and there is no light of day. It is painful to speak of. From now on, the most important issue in Shaanxi is famine relief. If you have not been there in person, you will never know the depth of the suffering of the people of Shaanxi. The central government will definitely find a way to save them in the future. I also hope that philanthropists at home and abroad will pay special attention to the Shaanxi disaster and raise huge sums of money to save these starving people."

Recent War Situation Near Nanning

Outbreak of Three-pronged War in the Upper Reaches of the Dahe River; Guangdong Air Force Continuously Bombs Nanning

A Guangzhou dispatch reports that the war situation in Nanning, Guangxi Province, has recently become tense again. According to front-line news, the Zhang-Gui army fears that the Central Army will reinforce Guangxi, so they are taking this opportunity to make a final struggle. In recent days, most of the Zhang-Gui army in Nanning has gathered there. It is estimated that the 11th Division of Zhang Fakui's troops and two regiments of Huang Heling's troops are stationed outside the East Gate of Nanning City. At the Lu Gong Ancestral Hall and Gao'ao north of the city, there are three regiments of Wei Yunsong's troops. In Xixiangtang west of the city, there is the Independent Regiment directly under Li Zongren and two battalions of Huang Xuchu's troops. In Shanglin, Wuming and other places, there are three regiments of Yang Tenghui's troops. The above-mentioned troops are mixed and dispatched, with Li Shouren as the chief commander at the front and Zhang Fakui as the deputy commander. On the first day of this month, they advanced towards the 8th and 10th Route Armies in four directions. Yang Tenghui and Huang Xuchu's troops intercepted the 10th Route Yunnan Army at Nalong. A fierce battle broke out between the two sides in Wuming. The Yunnan Army's Zhang Chong Division resisted bravely, and the Gui army suffered heavy casualties and retreated to Dahe. The Zhang-Gui army also advanced in three directions, with the remnants of Zhang Fakui's troops taking the central route, moving from Shanglin to the Bin Yang position of the 8th Route Army. The number of people was about 2,000. They were met head-on by the Ye Zhao Brigade stationed in Bin Yang. After a fierce battle of about six hours, Yu Hanmou, the commander of the 59th Division of the 8th Route Army, immediately increased the support of the Peng Linsheng Department of the Teaching Regiment. The enemy suffered more than half of its losses and was defeated back to Qianjiang. The 59th Division followed up and captured many prisoners. At the same time, about 2,000 troops of the Gui army's right wing, Bai Chongxi's troops, invaded Yongchun and Hengxian on the morning of the 1st. The Yang Dingzhong Department and Zhu Weizhen Department of the newly编16th Division of the 8th Route Army stationed there rose up to meet them. The two sides were locked in intense combat. Later, the Huang Zhiqiu Brigade of the 63rd Division of the 8th Route Army arrived and defeated the Bai Chongxi and Wei Yunsong troops. Currently, the Huang Brigade is firmly defending Guixian as a rear support for Yang's division in Yongchun. At noon on the 1st, the left wing of the Gui army, led by Li Zongren, once again led the militia army from Liuzhou along Pingletu to attack Majiang. It is heard that this remnant force is Tang Shengming's Hunan Army, about 1,000 people. One to two thousand troops of Zhang Fakui's troops were recently transferred to Xiuren and Lipu, and it seems that they have a tendency to move towards the Fu River. The 8th Route Army is currently preparing to launch a large-scale attack on Nanning to first break the enemy's base and then divide its troops to attack Liuzhou, which will be easier to do. For the Fu River, they have decided to take a defensive posture. The Wuxing Camp has sent hundreds of water mines to the rear to be distributed along the defense line below Zhaoping and Mengshan. Two thousand taidao knives were also ordered to be made in the rear for each division to form a taidao knife team. Each division is equipped with a taidao knife team of about 150 people, specializing in charging and destroying the defensive lines of the enemy in southern Vietnam. It has also been decided that the air force team will launch a general attack on Nanning City. Starting from the 6th, bombs were dropped on Nanning. Today (the 7th), Captain Hu Jinya led the Zhongshan, Nanhai, Taishan, Zhujiang, Panyu, Nanxiong, Dongguan, Yingde, Qujiang, and Changjiang planes, carrying powerful bombs, to Nanning to bomb the enemy. The 8th Route Army headquarters has prepared 100,000 yuan in relief funds for the future relief of bombed residents. On the army side, the Li Yangjing Department of the 63rd Division will be the vanguard of the attack on Nanning, with the Yang Dingzhong Department of the 16th Division as the reserve team. The Huang Zhiwen Department of the 126th Brigade under Li's division will coordinate with Yang's division to advance from Guixian along the Dahe River towards Yongchun County to attack the flank of Nanning City. The Huang Yanhuan Department of the 125th Brigade will join the Huang Renhuan Brigade of Yu Hanmou's division to attack the front of Nanning from Binyang via Santang. (November 7th)

Ruan Zhaochang Leads Troops to Jiangxi

A Wuhu dispatch reports that after the Jiangxi bandits were surrounded by the Central Army, they suddenly disturbed the border of Anhui. The Huizhou region is very nervous, and Qiupu even fell. The telegraph poles and wires of the county and Wangjiang and Anqing were also destroyed by bandits. In addition to Anqing sending a portion of its troops to deal with the situation, Chen Tiaoyuan also ordered the special task force of Hao Jiajun, which was stationed in Datong, to go to suppress the bandits. Now, Ruan Zhaochang of the 55th Division has also been ordered to lead all of his troops to the border of Anhui and Jiangxi to assist the armies of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi in preventing and surrounding the bandits. The 163rd Brigade of the division has already departed from Datong to the vicinity of Huizhou and Qimen. The 164th Brigade of Li Songshan, which is stationed in Wuhu, has also been continuously transporting troops to Anqing for the past two days, taking the route through Wangjiang to advance towards the Jiangxi border. Division Commander Ruan, with his troops having fully departed, specially took the Jiang'an ship this morning to lead the division headquarters and directly subordinate artillery and engineering battalion troops to the province. The local security of Wuhu and various counties in southern Anhui is still being handled by the Xu Guoting Regiment stationed in Wuhu by the 57th Division. Because Xu is responsible as the commander of the 6th Bandit Suppression Zone, Xu also believes that the bandit disasters in Xuan City, Guangde, Langxi and other counties have been very serious recently, and the bandits in Langguang have gathered to more than a thousand people. In order to fundamentally eliminate them, a comprehensive plan must be made. Especially today (10th), he summoned the county magistrates of the 11 counties under the jurisdiction of the 6th District, including Nanling, Xuan City, Dangtu, Guangde, and Fanchang, to hold a bandit suppression conference at the command headquarters. More than 20 people, including the county magistrates and representatives of the counties, attended the meeting. Commander Xu presided over the meeting, and first the counties reported on the situation of the bandits, and then decided on the following measures: (1) Each joint county shall formulate a method for joint patrols and draw maps according to the terrain to jointly handle the matter. (2) The command headquarters shall order the local officials and gentry of each county to earnestly recruit villagers to serve as guides for bandit suppression. (3) The command headquarters shall strictly order each county to check the household registration within a time limit to purify the source of bandits. (4) The command headquarters shall formulate sleeve badges, passwords, and identification flags and issue them to each county for unification. (10th)

Tianjin-Longhai Railways Begin Reorganization

The Ministry of Railways Sends Personnel to Inspect the Tianjin-Pukou and Longhai Lines; Sectional Train Service

A Xuzhou dispatch reports that the Tianjin-Pukou and Longhai Railways were in the midst of the recent military affairs, and now that the military operations have ended, the transportation headquarters of the two railways have also been revoked. Although traffic has been restored, the railway administration is still in the process of reorganization. The recent situation is recorded as follows:

Tianjin-Pukou Railway: Since the Tianjin-Pukou Railway resumed direct through traffic on the 1st of this month, traffic has been relatively smooth. However, many vehicles were stored on other lines during the war, so in addition to the daily express trains and the four weekly round-trip Pingpu trains, short-distance ticket trains have not yet resumed, and there are also few carriages attached to each ticket train, and passengers are very crowded. Freight vehicles are also in short supply. The Xuzhou Transportation Association had a conflict with the railway over this issue last month, declaring a suspension of freight transportation and requesting instructions from the Ministry of Railways, which has now been fortunately resolved. It is heard that there are now only more than 200 vehicles and more than 20 locomotives on the entire railway. The Ministry of Railways sent Counselor Liang Hancao and Deputy Director Zhu Lvyun to take the Pingpu train north from Pupu on the evening of the 8th and passed through Xuzhou on the morning of the 9th. According to the talks, they went to Jinan and Tianjin to inspect the railway conditions. It is likely that they will need to contact the Tianjin office. The railway bureau also sent Xu Ruitian, Chen Mengruo, and Liu Yimin and others to go west through Xuzhou on the 9th to investigate the vehicles stored on the Longhai Railway in preparation for transporting them back for reorganization to benefit transportation.

Longhai Railway: The entire Longhai Line has been opened to traffic, but it is operated in sections. On the western section, three or four trains run between Xuzhou and Zhengzhou, five or six trains run between Bian and Luo, and seven or eight trains run between Luo and Shaanxi. The roadbed on the western road has been damaged year after year and has not been thoroughly repaired, and there are also few vehicles. According to investigations, there are a total of more than 300 vehicles and about 30 locomotives on the entire railway, and most of them are occupied by the military, resulting in extremely crowded passengers on each ticket train. It is currently determined that the special express train between Xuzhou and Zhengzhou will resume from the 10th, with a planned round trip of twice a week. It is unknown whether this can be achieved. The wages of railway employees from Lanfeng to Lingbao have been in arrears for seven months. The railway bureau has only issued the salary for the most recent month, and the remaining arrears must be submitted to the Ministry of Railways for handling. As for the unfinished road construction west of Lingbao, it has not yet been possible to start continuous repairs. The location of the management bureau has also not been determined. From a business perspective, it is appropriate in Xuzhou; from a road construction perspective, it is appropriate in Zhengzhou. (9th)

Shandong Commercial Bank Will Resume Business

A Jinan dispatch reports that the former Shandong Commercial Bank had the oldest qualifications among the banks in Jinan City and was the tacit leader of the province's economic circles. In the spring of the 17th year, it collapsed due to Zhang Zongchang's excessive borrowing of funds. The Yumaogongli Money Bureau and various banks were also affected and collapsed. The city's financial situation was greatly affected. At the time of the bank's collapse, more than 800,000 yuan of banknotes were issued, falling to 20% of their face value. In the spring of the 18th year, in order to maintain the resumption of the bank's business, creditors (those with deposits) and noteholders (those with the bank's banknotes) decided to order the bank to resume business on July 1st of the 18th year, with banknotes redeemed in five years and deposits repaid in ten years. Just after the agreement was reached, the provincial government moved from Tai'an to Jinan. The former Director of Industry and Commerce, Chen Luanshu, believed that the bank's internal affairs were complicated and must be cleared up first. Therefore, it was decided that the Industry and Commerce Department, the creditor party, the noteholder party, and the capital party (the bank's directors) should organize a commercial bank clearing office to clear up all the bank's debts, claims, and property. The clearing committee consisted of three people from the Industry and Commerce Department and two committee members from each of the other three parties, for a total of nine people. Although the clearing work was interrupted by the Jin army entering Jinan and other incidents, it has not been suspended. As of now, it has been completed. It is estimated that 800,000 yuan of banknotes were issued by the bank, and 600,000 yuan have been recovered and stored with cut corners. The remaining unrecovered banknotes are no more than 200,000 yuan. The debts are about 1 million yuan, and the claims are also 1 million yuan, which can be offset. In addition, the bank also has several properties, and the directors Song Biru, Ji Zhiting, and others have raised 300,000 yuan and recruited 200,000 yuan of new shares, totaling 500,000 yuan. After discussing with the creditor party and the noteholder party, the bank will resume business immediately. Deposits will be repaid in five years, with 20% of the deposits repaid annually for the first four years and all deposits repaid in the fifth year. This plan has been reported to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines, and the Ministry of Agriculture has approved the bank to raise capital in cash and wait for personnel to check and verify it. If there is indeed a fund of 500,000 yuan, it will be allowed to resume business. The directors are now raising capital in preparation for verification, and the bank can resume business as late as January 1st next year. The market price of the bank's banknotes has now risen from 20% to 42% of their face value. (November 10th)

Qiupu County, Anhui Province, Harassed by Bandits

Occupied for Three Days and Recovered Immediately

An Anqing dispatch reports that Qiupu County, 130 miles from the provincial capital, has been repeatedly harassed by bandits. Last month, Pengze County, Jiangxi Province, was captured by the communist bandits led by Fang Zhimin. Qiupu was panicked because it was close to Pengze. Later, the Fang bandits withdrew from Pengze and fled to the mountains, planning to enter Anhui. The county repeatedly requested troops from the provincial government. The provincial government then consulted with Yue Shengxuan, the commander of the 57th Division, and sent Yan Heling's 139th Regiment to Dongliu to suppress the bandits as appropriate. However, on the 21st of last month, the Fang bandits had fled from Xiaojialing in Jiangxi to Longquanwan in Qiupu. The original security team in Longquanwan had more than 30 people. This time, because the bandits were outnumbered, the team leader Fan Zhanyuan and squad leader Liu Youzhang and team members Ding Shichun and Zhao Chunfang were all shot and killed. The bandits then occupied Longquanwan and planned to enter Chenjia Alley. The Chenjia Alley People's Self-Defense Corps tried their best to block them. Fortunately, Yan's regiment arrived in Qiupu and immediately advanced to attack. The bandits could not support themselves and retreated to Shimen Street and other places. At the beginning of this month, Yan's regiment was ordered to be transferred to defend against bandits. On the 4th night at 11 o'clock, the bandits took the opportunity to occupy Longquanwan and captured the Qiupu County seat. County Chief Du and representatives from all walks of life went to the provincial government to request assistance. Provincial Chairman Chen Tiaoyuan, who had just arrived in Anhui from Beijing, heard the news and immediately dispatched troops from the 55th Division to suppress the bandits. At 3 am on the 7th, Qiupu was recovered. The bandits were defeated and fled back to the mountains of Jiangxi. Although the bandits occupied the county for only three days, the local losses were enormous. County Chief Du has now joined forces with people from all walks of life to handle the aftermath. (November 10th)

Yan Xishan Returns to Wutai from Taiyuan

Secret Talks with Shang Zhen in Huangzhai Before Leaving; Yan's Camp Office Has Been Closed, But the Jin Army's Transfer of Defenses Is Still Very Busy

A Taiyuan dispatch on the 5th reports that since Liang Ruzhou and Wen Shouquan, representatives sent by Yan to the Northeast, arrived in Shenyang, they have been reporting the progress of the consultations by telegram every day. Although the outside world cannot know the details, according to internal sources, Liang and Wen have visited Zhang several times and have negotiated considerable guarantees for Yan's safety in WeChat. Yan then decided to retire. At 9 am on the 4th, he left the headquarters and went straight back to his original residence in Hebian Village, Wutai. Reporters stationed in other places, believing that Yan had prepared to step down, telegraphed reports today. When the telegrams were sent to the liaison section of the camp for inspection, the staff of the section believed that this matter was of great importance and could not be decided. Later, the telegrams were sent to Hebian for Yan's personal review and asked whether the telegrams could be sent. Yan immediately approved the word "send" after reading the telegrams. It was not until the evening that the telegrams were taken back from Hebian. According to headquarters sources, Yan's return to his hometown this time was very secret in advance, and even his close associates did not know. Yan went to the provincial government alone at about 9 am this morning. At that time, Provincial Chairman Shang Zhen was talking with two representatives of the Chambers of Commerce of various counties on the financial meeting. Yan stepped forward and took Shang's hand and whispered, "Follow me." Shang followed Yan out and boarded Yan's No. 1 car. Shang's empty car followed behind the No. 1 car. All the attendants and bodyguards were not taken. Only the car driver and three people followed and immediately drove straight out of the North Gate. When they arrived near Huangzhai (about sixty miles from the city), Yan ordered the car to stop and went to a small hilltop with Shang. The two sat on the ground and had a secret talk for a long time before Yan took the car north. Shang also got in the car and returned to the city. Yan will not come back within the most recent period of his return to his hometown.

There have been several rumors about the military and political leaders after Yan's stepping down. Some say it will be Xu Yongchang and Yang Aiyuan, and some say it will be Zhao Daiwen or Shang Zhen. There are many discussions, and it is impossible to come to a conclusion. But since Fu Zuoyi suddenly came to Taiyuan, it is generally said that Fu will be the most promising in the future. In short, it is difficult to make a definite statement before the official announcement. After receiving Yan's order to rush to complete the closing, Zhang Zhijie, the director of the camp's office, believed that the aftermath issues were also very important. He drafted the plan and submitted it to Yan for approval. All group members with a monthly salary of more than 100 yuan were recorded as recommended positions, and those with a monthly salary of less than 100 yuan were recorded as county clerk positions. Interns are appointed by the various departments. The headquarters of the Special Party Department has ordered the first and second propaganda teams and the cavalry propaganda team to immediately stop their work and cancel the names of the teams. All party affairs workers of the various armies will first return to the training department to wait for further assignments.

After Yan Xishan issued the telegram of stepping down on the 4th, he went to Hebian Village to express no thorough statement on the future aftermath of the Jin army. The Jin army has been transferring defenses in recent days and is very busy. Defenses have been deployed in the east, south, and north of Jin Province, and it seems that they have not abandoned the plan to maintain the entire Jin army. Although a portion of Feng Pengzhu's troops stationed in Huolu on the Zhengtai Road have withdrawn from the Jingxing Niangziguan area, the 25th Division is still waiting for orders in Huolu and has not yet expressed a willingness to cede the defense. However, the former enemy headquarters of the Jin army has returned the reporters and telegraph machines that were used to call the former Hebei Telegraph Administration for cancellation orders.

The Truth About the Anti-Japanese Resistance of the People of Taiwan

A Shantou dispatch reports that the people of Taiwan rose up to fight the Japanese this time, using the iron and blood of thousands of people to deal with the large Japanese army. Their spirit of sacrifice is truly admirable. However, most of the news about the beginning of this incident came from Japanese communication agencies, which are inevitably biased. I received a letter from Taiwan yesterday, which describes the cause and effect of this matter in great detail. I have recorded it below for the reference of readers.

Last year, the water of the Zhuoshui River in Taichung was clear for three days. The people of the whole island were quite bewildered, because the Zhuoshui River has never been clear. The elders said that when the water of the muddy river is clear, disaster will definitely occur, and the historical records are consistent with this. This spring, red rain suddenly fell near the area, covering an area of ​​six zhang long and wide. The people of Taiwan were even more surprised and believed that the coming of disaster was a sign from heaven. Unexpectedly, the change that occurred was a revolutionary war that had been suppressed for a long time. The cause of this matter was that the Taiwanese people, who were regarded as savages by the Japanese, numbered more than 130,000. Because of the different terrains and races, they were divided into hundreds of tribes. Usually, each tribe was treated unfairly by the local government and suffered greatly. However, they were afraid of the strict Japanese police system and dared not launch a revolt. There was a Taiwanese clan in Taichung Prefecture called Mengmai (transliteration), and their village was called Wushe. This tribe was the most civilized of the Taiwanese tribes. When the Japanese entered Taiwan, the tribe was the first to surrender. It is said that their bloodline is a mixture of Dutch and local aborigines. The population is about 2,000 people, and there are only more than 500 strong men. Most of the people in the tribe have received Japanese education and have good culture and knowledge. The eldest son of the tribe's leader, named Hanoka Ichiro, was a handsome young man with a fearless revolutionary spirit. He graduated from Taichung Normal School. After graduation, he originally planned to become a teacher so that he could use education to promote his revolutionary work. However, the Japanese government knew that he was talented and capable and did not allow him to change his position to become a policeman to manage the tribe. Since Hanaoka's ambition was not fulfilled, he turned to谋 other changes and conspired with the people in the tribe on a revolutionary plan, making organized and prepared launches. Everything was properly arranged, so they purchased food one month in advance and moved the children to other tribes a few days before the incident to avoid being trampled on. Thus, the war opened. It was found that the tribe cut off the traffic and telephone lines in various places on the 26th of last month, leaving only the most important ones uncut to hide the ears and eyes of the Japanese. On the 27th, it happened to be the joint sports meeting of various elementary schools in Wushe. All the police chiefs and students gathered. The tribe divided into two teams to attack, one team went to the police branch to cut off the phone and seize more than 150 guns, more than 50,000 bullets, and countless gunpowder. On that day, many Japanese police families were also killed, which shows the deep resentment of the Taiwanese people against the Japanese. One team drove to the sports field to attack. It is estimated that about 200 people were killed, all of whom were Japanese. Taiwanese and Han Chinese were not harmed. Their goals were clear. After the incident, the whole Taiwan was shocked, and the Japanese immediately dispatched troops to respond to the enemy. On the 28th, they began to dispatch police forces and troops from all over the country, totaling more than 2,000 people, and five planes arrived on the 31st to launch a general attack. The commander of the Japanese army was Kamata. Because the Taiwanese people of Wushe were fighting effectively, they could not be taken lightly. He moved his headquarters to the combat area, as serious as confronting an enemy country. In a fierce battle until the 2nd of this month, although the Japanese army occupied several mountain ridges of the other side, the dangerous places were still difficult to capture. The tribe's fighting skills were quite clever. They avoided the Japanese planes' bombing, hid during the day and went out at night, and were familiar with the path, either encircling or flanking, and were always victorious. Although the Japanese army had a large number of people, they were no match for them. Moreover, they were able to create a kind of firearm that was buried on the side of the road and tied the fire line to the center of the road. When the Japanese army passed through the area and accidentally touched the fire line, tens of thousands of crossbows were fired at the same time, and no one was spared. The Japanese army was once ambushed and suffered more than a dozen casualties. Because the tribe lived in the mountains and made a living by hunting, they were very accurate in firing guns and extremely fast in walking in the mountains. When competing with the Japanese army, the Japanese army sighed that they were not as good as them. Since this matter was transmitted to Tokyo, the Japanese government has attached great importance to it and specially sent Mr. Komae, the Director of the National Savage Bureau, to Taiwan to inspect the situation and bring two missions: 1. Do not deal with the enemy with the methods of hatred and revenge. 2. Punish criminal savages within the scope of the law. It is feared that once other tribes are mistakenly killed, it will provoke public outrage throughout Taiwan and cause the war to expand day by day, which is not a good strategy.

Unexpectedly, on the 1st of this month, the Japanese army had mistakenly killed a member of another Taiwanese tribe, and the tribe was also angry and wanted to move. The Japanese were very afraid and immediately dispatched more than 30 troops and local police to suppress the situation. The situation is becoming more and more serious. Anyone who knows the situation in Taichung believes that this incident cannot be taken lightly, because the Taiwanese people deeply sympathize with the Wushe action. As for the rumors that the women of Wushe committed suicide to encourage their husbands and sons to fight to the death, it is a one-sided statement by the Japanese. It is heard that more than 100 women in the tribe were killed by the Japanese. The Japanese were afraid that people would say that they were indiscriminately killing people who had no resistance, so they blamed it on suicide. (November 8th)

Kidnapping Case in Xiaofeng Alley; Limited Time to Solve the Case. The home of Feng Yunsheng, the deputy chief of the fourth (Kaiyuan Township) Xiaofeng Alley Shuiqu township in the county was broken into by seven or eight bandits with guns at about 2:00 am on the 24th of September. However, the ransom ticket Feng Yuequan has not been captured and is still missing. County Chief Pan submitted a report to the public seeking instructions on how to handle the matter. He issued a reprimand yesterday and ordered him to set another deadline of half a month to strictly hunt down the bandits and rescue the ransom ticket.

Abuse of Wife Case; Accomplice Apprehended. Pan Sandai, a resident of Wanan City, District 16, and Phan Chai, a subordinate of the district in the same location, became acquainted with his widowed sister-in-law and then called on the local hooligan Pan Wubao to beat his wife, Zhang'e, severely and lock her tightly on the coffin of her father. Zhang Jilin, Zhang'e's brother, requested the Public Security Bureau to order the police to go to the countryside to arrest them. Rugao

Living Burial Incident in Dujiazhuang Feng Jun, a farmer from Dujiazhuang in the Chema Lake District, was sunning grass in the field the other day when, for some reason, a neighbor, Du Sanbuzhi, gathered Zhu Lian, Chen Xikou, Fei Zhu, and others, who beat him and buried him alive. Fortunately, passersby heard cries and dug him out, saving him from death. A special report was filed.

After questioning by the chief of the local Public Security Sub-bureau, the case was submitted to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation. Yesterday afternoon, the Bureau Chief conducted a preliminary hearing. According to Du San's testimony, Feng Jun struck his wife's leg with a willow branch, causing her immediate pain. Du San refused to accept this and fought back, admitting to burying Feng in the earth. Zhu Lian and Chen Xikou testified that they participated in the beating and burial. Fei Zhu stated that he did not participate in the beating and burial, but helped cover the body with soil in the field. Based on the testimony, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau deemed the case a major crime involving the attempted murder of a human life. All involved witnesses were transferred to the county for trial.

One Old Woman's Words Result in Four Deaths A certain family in Baihu Town West had a daughter seven years ago, whom they cherished greatly. Recently, they had a son. A neighbor, an old woman surnamed So-and-So, jokingly said to the daughter, "From now on, your parents will favor sons over daughters!" Unexpectedly, after hearing this, the daughter cut off her brother's genitals and presented them to her father. Upon seeing this, the father was overwhelmed with grief and hanged himself. The mother, upon discovering this, was filled with anger and tore the daughter to pieces, then threw herself into the river. It was truly a tragic scene.

Jiading

Chrysanthemum Exhibition The County Public Education Center held a calligraphy and painting exhibition and chrysanthemum show at the center's public lecture hall last year to commemorate the anniversary of the passing of Sun Yat-sen. The center has decided to continue this event this year. A preparatory committee was formed, and famous calligraphers and painters, as well as rare and unique chrysanthemums from various chrysanthemum growers, were gathered for a five-day exhibition from the 12th to the 16th.

Pinghu

Opium Headquarters Busted Yesterday (the 10th) at 9:00 AM, Yang Zhuqing, the patrol captain of the County Government, acting on the secret orders of County Magistrate Shen, went to the residence of Li Zhanglin in Xiang Lane to search for opium. Yang immediately sent plainclothes detectives to investigate, and then led the police to the house. Zhanglin was not home. Li's hired hand, Ni Tongsheng, and Li's mistress, were arrested and brought to the county. A total of over one hundred ten packages of dried opium paste, over one hundred packages of copper coins in a wooden box, thirty yuan in silver dollars, and over six hundred dimes were confiscated. Captain Yang handed over the seized items to the patrol chief for safekeeping. At 1:00 PM, Trial Official Li, together with Yang Zhuqing, inventoried the evidence, which was brought to the county.

Educational News

Important News

Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office Rectifies Tax Collection

Former Yixing Finance Bureau Chief Performed Poorly, Province Requested Disciplinary Action According to Law

The Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office sent an official letter to the Provincial Government regarding the poor performance of Tan Xiangqi, the former Yixing Finance Bureau Chief, and current Taixing Finance Bureau Chief, requesting disciplinary action according to law. The letter reads: We have investigated the case of Tan Xiangqi, the former Yixing Finance Bureau Chief and current Taixing Finance Bureau Chief, who misappropriated over 32,200 yuan of provincial education funds during his tenure in Yixing. Successive chiefs have shifted responsibility, delaying resolution. We have repeatedly ordered and urged the current Finance Bureau Chief, Li Jianding, to work together to submit a telegram stating that the funds will be included in the local budget starting in the 20th year and repaid over three years. Currently, the provincial education funds rely on borrowed funds, creating incomparable difficulties. This autumn, the county has experienced a bountiful harvest, and the winter grain shipments are about to begin. If this large sum is not deducted and resolved during this peak collection period, but instead is deferred to the 20th year's budget for repayment over three years, this slow approach will not alleviate the urgent situation. We have instructed the bureau to reconvene a meeting and devise a plan to repay the full amount as quickly as possible, subject to review. We are concerned that this may not be followed. Chief Tan Xiangqi has already made mistakes in the past and has not thought to improve in the future. His transfer to the Taixing Finance Bureau has resulted in even worse performance. The report form submitted for the first ten days of May understated the amount of harvest tax collected by 167 taels, 6 mace, 2 fen, and 1 li. We discovered this and ordered a review, which he attributed to a clerical error. Taxes are of utmost importance, yet he seemed unaware of the oversight. How can he be held responsible? Previous chiefs in Taixing cleared taxes on a monthly basis. Since this chief took office, taxes have been in arrears for as many as seven months. Not only has he ignored repeated urgings, but he recently initiated a joint petition from various counties to defer the allocation of harvest tax funds until the end of the 19th year's settlement. How can the monthly expenses of the schools be met if they have to wait until the end of the year for disbursement? These absurd statements and the delayed resolution of the Yixing debt are consistent. The petition also states that other counties have not yet demarcated [funds], so where does this assertion come from? This is incomprehensible. All of the above demonstrates that the chief is trifling with important public affairs and disregarding provincial orders. The real situation cannot be concealed. Our office has the responsibility but not the authority to directly remove and punish. However, if such a negligent chief cannot be subject to disciplinary action according to the law, then taxes from each county can be withheld at will. Regulations would become mere formalities, and demarcation would be a waste of time. The shortfall in education revenue would be impossible to investigate, and there would be no need for office management. Would this not clearly violate the late Premier's clear instruction to protect independence? The seeds of disaster have been sown, and the issue persists. We must make this solemn declaration. In addition to informing the Department of Finance for reference, we also request your government to investigate. Please consider the extreme difficulties faced by provincial schools and provide effective assistance. Swiftly subject Chief Tan Xiangqi to disciplinary action, immediately remove him from office, and make a public announcement to deter others. This will ensure the proper use of funds for education and benefit the public. Sincerely, Niu Yongjian, to the Jiangsu Provincial Government.

China Public School Disturbance, Hu Shih and Wang Yunwu Arrive to Urge Resumption of Classes

Ma Junwu Returns from Japan

(National News Agency) The report that China Public School Principal Yu Youren arrived at the school on the 10th to maintain order was published in yesterday's paper. It is now known that the delegation organized by the "Welcoming Ma Faction" sealed off all the classrooms and the entire student body went on strike. The details are as follows:

Welcoming Ma Faction Situation The members of the "Welcoming Ma Faction" at the school are mostly students from Guangdong and Guangxi. They elected representatives to form a delegation, which established an office in classroom number 8. They have used over 700 yuan in student association fees and organized a disciplinary team to post slogans and distribute flyers to implement a forceful resolution. Most students are intimidated by them, daring to be angry but not daring to speak out. The "Welcoming Yu Faction" is trying to avoid conflict with the delegation. The two sides have exchanged flyers and posters and have had several scuffles, which were resolved by the military police without any major injuries.

Zhang Yaoguang Arrested Zhang Yaoguang is the leader of the delegation and the closest student to Professor Luo Longji. When Luo Longji was arrested, Zhang personally escorted him to the car. Zhang then learned that he was also on the list of those to be arrested and went into hiding in Shanghai. Later, when Luo Longji was released on bail and returned to the school, Zhang also returned to Songjiang to work actively. However, in July of this year, he was arrested by the Seventh District Detective Squad of the Public Security Bureau and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He has not yet been released. The reason for Zhang Yaoguang's arrest is that he is in charge of the Nationalist faction at the school.

Welcoming Yu Faction Situation The "Welcoming Yu Faction" is sympathetic to the general student body. However, because the school authorities protect the "Welcoming Ma Faction" and suppress the "Welcoming Yu Faction", it is unable to conduct its activities as openly as the "Welcoming Ma Faction". Its true strength is difficult to determine. However, based on the situation when Mr. Yu arrived at the school to maintain order, it is known that everyone except for 30 to 40 members of the "Welcoming Ma Faction" welcomed Mr. Yu. Previously, the "Welcoming Ma Faction" spread the rumor that Mr. Yu would never come to the school and that the board of directors was using Mr. Yu as a transitional figure behind the scenes, so they temporarily kept silent. Later, seeing that Mr. Yu was indeed willing to come to the school to maintain order, the atmosphere changed. They are now eagerly hoping that Mr. Yu will return to the school after the Fourth Plenary Session and officially take office.

League of Allies Representation The League of Allies is an organization within the "Welcoming Yu Faction". This time, the welcoming of Mr. Yu was initiated by the League. The other night, they sent representatives to Mr. Yu to express their views. Mr. Yu said that he had to attend the Fourth Plenary Session and would handle the matter after it closed. Currently, members of the League of Allies are remaining calm and awaiting Mr. Yu's return to the school for his disposition.

School Suddenly Goes on Strike After Mr. Yu arrived at the school and expressed his responsibility, all the students were relieved. Seeing that the situation was turning against them, the "Welcoming Ma Faction" plotted a final show of force. The other day, Wang Hongshi (Director of General Affairs) handed over the keys to the delegation, which sealed off all the classrooms and forced the students to go on strike. The professors were unaware of this beforehand and arrived at the school carrying their briefcases. Seeing the situation, they all left carrying their briefcases.

Ma Did Not Arrive at School Yesterday The report that Ma Junwu returned to Shanghai the other day was published in yesterday's paper. After hearing the news, the school's delegation sent out several notices overnight, saying that Mr. Ma was scheduled to arrive at the school at 10 AM yesterday and that the students were to gather at the main parade ground at 9 AM to go to the Paotaiwan train station to welcome him. However, they suddenly received a verbal notice from Mr. Ma saying that he had just returned from overseas and was extremely tired and unable to arrive as scheduled. The delegation immediately issued an emergency notice to dismiss the students. It is said that around 4 PM, Hu Shih and Wang Yunwu arrived at the school and reported that the students must resume classes immediately and that the principal matter would be resolved by the board of directors.

Hu Shih and Wang Yunwu Arrive at School to Give a Speech Another message states that after Ma Junwu arrived in Shanghai, representatives of the China Public School earnestly requested that he return to the school to preside over affairs. Mr. Ma originally intended to arrive at the school at 4 PM on the 12th, but was unable to do so due to his poor health. He entrusted Hu Shih and Wang Yunwu to bring a personal letter to the school to persuade the students to resume classes and await the board of directors' resolution. Students inside and outside the school were covered with posters welcoming Principal Ma and high-hanging welcome flags. At 3 PM, they gathered at the main parade ground and went to the Wusong River bank to welcome him. When the car arrived at the river bank, all the students set off firecrackers and clapped, cheering loudly. Hu Shih and Wang Yunwu got out of the car and explained that Mr. Ma could not arrive because of his poor health. The students immediately asked Hu and Wang to come to the school to give a speech. Hu Shih said that Mr. Ma could not return to the school because of his poor health. I represent Mr. Ma in apologizing to you and, in my capacity as a member of the board of directors, I would like to say a few words to you. Mr. Ma has a letter for me to bring to persuade you to resume classes and await the board of directors' resolution. That's also what I mean. I like your warm welcome of Mr. Ma very much. When I was president, I never received such a warm welcome from students. I am very jealous of your enthusiasm for Mr. Ma, but at the same time I am very happy because China Public School has such a president who can make me jealous, and that is the best thing. I will definitely tell all the directors about your enthusiasm for welcoming Mr. Ma. I will definitely help you with your request for Mr. Ma to return to his post. But now that you are on strike to await resolution, the loss is too great. I think it is better to wait while attending classes. If waiting while attending classes still does not solve the problem, then it is not too late to think of a solution. After Hu's speech, he asked the students for their opinions on the spot. Most of the students advocated for a strike to await resolution. Only after Hu repeatedly persuaded them did they temporarily agree to resume classes to await resolution. Finally, Wang Yunwu gave a speech that was roughly the same as Hu's.

Ma Junwu's Letter to All Students of China Public School To all students of China Public School: I am extremely grateful for your welcome upon my arrival in Shanghai yesterday. I am also grateful to know from your letters that the students hope that Junwu will come to the school immediately. Junwu also very much wants to meet with you, but recently returned and all issues are still under consideration, so it is not convenient to speak at this time. However, I sincerely hope that all students will resume classes immediately to avoid great losses in their studies. As for the school's problems, you should wait patiently for the board of directors to resolve them. I deeply hope that all students will understand this intention. Ma Junwu, October 12

Sports

Basketball Star Zhao Renming Passes Away

The Sports Community Mourns Together, Memorial Game to Be Held

Mr. Zhao Renming, the eldest son of Zhao Jiechu, a Shanghai tea merchant, graduated from Fudan University in 1924. He was known for his integrity, cheerful disposition, and elegance. He studied diligently while at school and was consistently at the top of his class. He excelled in sports, especially basketball. He served as the basketball representative of the Youth Association, the birthplace of Shanghai basketball talent, the basketball representative of the middle school, and the captain of the Fudan University basketball team, which won the Jiangnan University championship in 1924. In 1924, he was the captain of the East China basketball team that attended the Third National Games in Wuchang. He was a member of the Quanbai team, which won the Shanghai Basketball Championship for two consecutive years from 1923 to 1925, and a member of the Qingguang team, which won the Shanghai Championship in 1928. Unfortunately, he passed away from typhoid fever at Longhua Hospital at 6 PM on the 8th of this month. Mr. Zhao was known for his wide circle of friends and amiable personality. The sports community was saddened and grieved by the news of his death. It is said that his close friend, Mr. Tan, plans to gather famous basketball players in Shanghai and hold a grand competition with the Qingnianhui team (which had the best record last year) or other teams of comparable strength. All proceeds from ticket sales will be donated to charity in memory of their late friend. In life, Mr. Zhao was friendly to famous basketball players in the basketball community and there will be no shortage of supporters for this event. Although this event is an unprecedented innovation in the Shanghai sports community, it is also a means of raising money at a time when there are widespread disaster victims, and Mr. Zhao can rest in peace in the afterlife knowing that this occurred.

Municipal Elementary School Joint Sports Meet Day One

Yesterday marked the opening of the third joint sports meet for elementary schools in Shanghai. The weather cleared up after a long period of rain, and the athletes and spectators were refreshed. The situation is recorded as follows:

Opening Ceremony

Each elementary school arrived one after another starting at 8:00 AM. The marching formation took some time, so the music started at 9:30 AM. The ceremony was conducted as usual. Director Xu Peihuang of the Education Bureau reported on the purpose of the meeting and the preparations. Then, a representative of the Municipal Party Committee, Mr. Tong Xingbai, gave a speech. Then, the sports meet song was sung, led by musician Zhong Zitong. After the marching formation, the sports began.

Grand Marching Formation

The number of people was over two thousand four hundred, arranged in order according to the symbols marked on the ground, which was quite neat and orderly. The position of general commander was held by Wang Huaiqi, and the sound of the order to mount and issue orders was like a thunderclap. The movements of the elementary school students were also very neat and lively, all of which were well trained.

Chairman's Report

Mr. Xu said, "Today is the opening day of the third joint sports meet for elementary schools in this city, and it is also the anniversary of the Premier's birthday. Now I will give a brief report on the significance of holding the sports meet today and the preparation process. The purpose of our party's program is to realize the Three People's Principles, and the realization of the Three People's Principles has the greatest significance for physical health, because physical health is the only way to strive to build a common construction so that the Three People's Principles of nation, democracy and people's livelihood can all be completely resolved. The Premier's writings and lectures during his lifetime often show the importance of physical education and the benefits of sports to our people. The joint elementary school sports meet of our city has begun in the previous and current sessions on the anniversary of the Premier's birth. The purpose is to let everyone commemorate the Premier's birthday and to let everyone practice the Premier's legacy of paying attention to physical education. In other words, the physique of the people of China today is far inferior to that of the ancients. The ancients were tall and big, and today's people are short and small. By the way, the Japanese people used to be short and small, but now they are gradually growing taller, and their spirit is also extremely full. This is clear evidence that sports can improve the body. Compared to the many children in front of me, I am afraid that they are not as good as Japanese elementary school students in terms of physique and spirit. Compared to European and American children, the difference is even greater. Therefore, the purpose of holding the joint elementary school sports meet is to cultivate the will to work hard to exercise one's physique, and secondly, to cultivate the spirit of unity. Dr. Sun Yat-sen said that the 400 million compatriots of China are like a plate of broken sand, but how can we unite them? We must pay attention to training from an early age. We are putting thousands of elementary school students together to hold a sports meet for this purpose. Next is to cultivate rational competition. No matter what kind of business, solid unity and rational competition will lead to victory. All the world's powers pay attention to this point. I hope that the performances of each school are the true results of ordinary efforts, not the false results of temporary excitement. Winning certainly requires further progress, and even if you lose, you must continue to exercise and strive for future success. This is rational competition. As for the schools participating in this session, there are a total of eighty-four, including sixty-one municipal schools and twenty-three private schools. There are more than 890 male students participating in track and field, more than 410 female students participating in track and field, more than 2,410 people in the grand march, and about 150 group performances, with an estimated total of over 5,000 people. The sports are divided into three parts: track and field, gymnastics, and national martial arts. Each part of the judges is invited to be a physical education expert who has no relationship with each school to show fairness. In addition to the staff of this bureau and the sports field, the preparations before the event were also supported by various schools and people from all walks of life, which is deeply appreciated.

Representative of the Municipal Party Committee Gives a Speech

Tong Xingbai said, "Today is the first day of the third joint sports meet for elementary schools in the city. I will tell you what I know as a representative of the Municipal Party Committee. We know that physical education is not only about exercising the body, but is the foundation of all education. The development of physical education not only makes the body of each individual healthy, but also makes the body of the whole nation healthy. Various undertakings will also develop and progress accordingly. If the foundation is not strong, how can wisdom, morality and education be achieved? Today, what I want to say is about the following points. (1) We must know that exercising the body is a permanent effort, not a temporary attention. Every school commits the mistake of moving for a prize, not for exercising the body. When the sports meet is approaching, they rush to practice. When the sports meet is over, they abandon it. What is the point of being exposed to the sun for one day and freezing for ten days? 2. Physical education is extremely important, but other subjects should not be abandoned due to physical education. There are a few schools that treat athletes as a special class, giving them convenience in class and exams, and giving them preferential treatment in food, clothing and living. This method is very unreasonable. 3. I hope that the elementary school physical education in the city will be systematically and uniformly developed. Now there are many different clothing colors in the field. I think that in the future, it will always be unified. It is not only the uniformity of form, but also the practical aspects of physical education must be unified to form the entire elementary school physical education in Shanghai."

Guests Attending

Yesterday, the guests attending the meeting included Zhu Yingpeng, a member of the Supervisory Committee of the Municipal Party Committee, as well as Zheng Xigu, Gu Zheng, Chen Zhang'e, Chen Jiaxuan, Chen Mengyu, Yu Yuanjue, Lu Lihua and dozens of others. More than 30,000 students from elementary schools and a large number of people from all walks of life came to visit, but the surrounding areas were already full of elementary school students and there was no room to stand.

Selection of Awards

In addition to more than a dozen woolen flags made by the conference itself and hundreds of medals of various colors, the awards that have been handed over to the conference and displayed on the stage include four large silver cups from Mayor Zhang and his wife, two silver shields from the Jingwu Physical Culture Association, a satin flag, a silver shield from the Municipal National Arts Museum, three satin flags from the MinGuo Daily News, a silver cup from the Xinwen Daily News, a velvet flag from the ShenBao Daily News, one vertical axis each for the men's and women's sections of the East Asia Sports School, two woolen flags from the China Sports School, a silver shield from Jinan University, and one velvet flag each from Zhu Yingpeng and Ma Chongkan, and a silver shield from Zheng Tan. A silver cup from the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, a silver shield from the Southeast Women's Physical Education School, a large flower ring from the Standard Sports Equipment Company, and ten woolen flags from the Brothers Store. It is said that the prizes from other institutions and individuals are still being rushed to produce.

Group Gymnastics Performance

Yesterday, there were a total of fifty-five group performances in the morning and afternoon. The most praised by the audience was the lively imitation ball exercises of the Wanzhu School, the natural and lovely singing expression of the Tangwan School's exercise imitations, and the brilliant and harmonious movements of the Chengzhong Affiliated Elementary School. But the score is lower to determine the merits of the team must be judged by gymnastics staff.

Yesterday, due to the grand assembly of two thousand several hundred people in the morning, entering and exiting the field took up much time. The track and field competition began around 11 a.m. The number of male and female students registered for each of the four running groups was quite large. Preliminary and semi-final rounds continued incessantly until sunset, resulting in the postponement of the 400-meter preliminary, 200-meter preliminary and semi-final, and 50-meter preliminary and semi-final. China Electric Football Team vs. Newspaper Workers

A Score of Three to Three

The friendship between the Huashang Electric Workers' Union and the press workers' union has always been known to be deep. After the match, both teams drove to the China Electric club for light refreshments and then dispersed. It is said that the two unions plan to hold a friendly table tennis match next week.
