Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas are cold and cloudy with light fog. There are strong northwest to northeast winds over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. The winds are even stronger in the Taiwan Strait. The weather is bad south of the Ogasawara Islands. Also, the highest temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 51.8 degrees, and the lowest was 31.8 degrees. The highest temperature on the same day last year was 58.8 degrees, and the lowest was 33.3 degrees.

Letter

To the editor: Recently, I read in your newspaper's news column on November 9th about the meeting of the tenants of Qingyun Lane, in which it was stated that Xing Dingcheng went to Zhenqinji Real Estate Company on Sichuan Road on September 10th to discuss important matters with his friend Gu Wensheng. However, after investigation, there is no person named Gu Wensheng in our company, and it is Zhenqin Real Estate Construction Company, not Zhenqin Real Estate Company. I am afraid there is a misunderstanding that affects our reputation. Therefore, I am writing to request that you publish this letter to correct the record. Sincerely, Zhenqin Real Estate Construction Company, November 12th.

Shanghai Market

Market News

At the beginning of the invention of the Zhongling Printing Machine, the National Government specially awarded a five-year patent exemption and a one-year tax exemption this month. Now that the tax exemption period has expired, the customs office will collect a one-time tax on the export of machine-made foreign goods. Yesterday, Niu Zaikun, a representative from Sichuan, and other members visited the Shanghai Hanli Factory and saw that the factory was well-equipped and manufactured high-quality products. Now that our country's industry is young and tender, it is necessary to give this model factory practical protection so that its development can compete with foreign goods. A proposal was submitted to the National Industry and Commerce Conference to exempt the Zhongling Printing Machine from taxes. It was approved by a majority of members. The results of the review showed that this case should be handled by the Hanli Company by submitting the invention components to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for verification, and then encouraging it according to the special industry incentive method.

The Chrysanthemum Planting Society of the Nanjing Road Municipal Government is hosted by Mr. Yu Shun'en, the owner of the plantation. Social News

Why Edison Said That Education in the Future Can Use Movies to Replace Books (Continued)

— Lecture by Dr. Wei Zhong

Frank Borzage has his own method. He directed the film "The River" and divided the entire film into three parts. Two parts have music but use subtitles instead of dialogue. The actor's body movements are arranged in such a way that their body movements reach the point where they are about to speak before the subtitles appear. Tomorrow we can check. I don't know how much knowledge this director has, but the films he directs can combine the actors' body movements with the subtitles in a relationship like biology, where there is body movement first and then speech. All speech comes from body movement. You can see it in the film. It's easier to see in Mary Duncan than in Charles Farrell.

The experience from the movie mentioned above can help you see that speech comes from the body. Then where do words come from? We use science to answer as follows: words come from speech. Books are nothing more than written words. Simply put, the relationship between speech, words, and books can be called words are words in the freezer, and books are words that have been chilled in the freezer. There is body first, then speech, then words, and then books. Without a body, there is no speech, without speech, there are no words, and without words, there are no books. Buying books is usually stealing, but the people who make books are people with a certain level of ability. They have to have a combined activity of the body before they can have a combined activity of the book. The words they speak become words and are then written into books. A book is one of the last parts. His words are the most complete expression of the body produced by the combination of his whole body from head to toe. The sum of body activities in the brain is the expression of the combined activity of the brain, which is speech. Without a brain, there is no speech. Because human beings have human brains, human beings have speech. Animal brains are not developed, so their speech is incomplete. But human speech is the expression of the center point of the whole. The combination of the whole is the brain. Without the whole, there is no brain, and if the whole is not put together, there is still no brain, according to science.

We have just used our movies to explain the origin of words, so we can now rely on this experience to explain what kind of perspective future education has on books.

You must not use other people's experiences or other people's thoughts unless you have your own experiences and your own thoughts. Replacing my own experiences and my own thoughts with other people's experiences and other people's thoughts is to kill my own experiences and my own thoughts.

In short, movies in the new education are long-lasting external stimuli. Movies combine things that are constantly moving. Why is the movie we are watching tomorrow called "The River"? Because it is a very moving movie. The most moving thing besides air is water. Tomorrow you can see how moving the water is flowing down from the high mountains of America.

Religious education gives you nouns, while scientific education gives you stimuli. It constantly stimulates you, not allowing you to doze off, not allowing you to be a Bodhisattva. Movies overthrow the people who are Bodhisattvas, the people who look down on the body. This is the greatest role of movies.

Look at the Chinese moralists and foreign believers. They all think that movies are external and inferior things. They think that they themselves are superior people and only want books. Only those inferior people will want external stimuli. They say, "You go to the cinema, it is much more important for us to go and buy books."

In fact, movies are compatible with the scientific perspective. When religious culture has not yet transitioned into scientific culture, movies can help us practice accepting external stimuli. Movies deliberately prepare people for external stimuli. If you are a bookworm of religious culture, you will not feel the external stimuli. Movies can make you feel the external stimuli and make you have to feel the external stimuli. This allows your body to gradually get the opportunity to practice receiving stimuli and gradually develop new brains, so that there will be a new culture in the future.

Our religious culture people will not look for stimuli. Movies can help us practice looking for them, and the stimuli of movies are easier to happen and help with the brain's revival because movies stimulate your senses – the senses (ears and eyes) that are closest to and most related to the brain. If the higher senses practice receiving stimuli first, then the nose, mouth, hands, feet, stomach, and genitals will follow. It is very dangerous if the ears and eyes are not active, but the nose, lungs, stomach, hands, feet, genitals, and other organs are active. Movies first give people's higher senses the practice of receiving stimuli, which is the beginning of giving people's whole body the practice of receiving stimuli. The whole body's failure to practice accepting external stimuli is equal to the brain's inability to feel stimuli. At this point, our lecture today is completely finished.

I hope that the people who are here listening to the lecture now will go to watch the movie tomorrow to prove what I just said about using movies to explain "the relationship between the body and speech." Do not watch the inferior parts of the movie first – men taking off their clothes and going into the water – these inferior stimuli are what ordinary people will not go into the water for. First, use the higher stimuli, first watch the higher parts, and then watch the inferior parts.

Youth Corner

The Bulletin Board Craze at Minli Middle School

Everyone knows that Minli Middle School is an old-fashioned school. Students' thoughts and actions are strictly limited. The bulletin board craze that broke out last week is enough to prove everything.

The "Minli Bulletin Board" was the first to be launched in the school. The newspaper used interesting, lively text and news to bring back the students' adjustment of the boring school life. Of course, there was no possibility of overstepping the scope.

However, the newspaper suffered a sudden misfortune at the beginning of its publication. This may have been implicated by the "Gecko" that was published at the same time. "The articles published in the Gecko are a collection of completely abusive criticisms of the school." Both newspapers were torn down by the school authorities one hour after they were posted. However, the "Minli Bulletin Board" was checked by the Department of Military Training and was stamped with an approved publication stamp.

After being torn down, it went through the review and misunderstanding of many faculty members of the school, and several conclusions were reached.

(1) Bulletin boards are also one of the student movements. Student movements should be prohibited.

(2) The people behind the Gecko and Minli Bulletin Board must be investigated.

Because running the bulletin board is to preside over the student movement.

(3) There is a short article in the Minli Bulletin Board titled "The Sharpening of the Fierce Battle between Nationalist Literature and Proletarian Literature." Because (1) it talks about Proletarian Literature, it is suspected of being communist.

However, is the fact exactly the same as what they think? I think it is not difficult for readers to imagine.

May I ask if the dozens of bulletin boards published by Fudan University have all violated the ban on student movements? Should all the organizers be investigated? What's even more ridiculous is the suspicion of communism. Mentioning Proletarian Literature in order to promote Nationalist Literature is suspected of being communist. Then, isn't the "Pioneer Weekly" and "Era Youth" and other publications that mention Proletarian Literature every issue even more suspected of being communist?

The waves of the bulletin board craze are still rising one by one, but the organizers do not dare to use clear and upright theories to defend themselves. (Ke)
